29/*



30 * Time delay interpolation routine



31 *



32 * The linear interpolation is performed using the formula:



33 *



34 *          (t2 - tMinusDelay)         (tMinusDelay - t1)



35 * u(t)  =  ----------------- * u1  +  ------------------- * u2



36 *              (t2 - t1)                  (t2 - t1)



37 */



38real_T rt_TDelayInterpolate(



39  real_T tMinusDelay,                  /* tMinusDelay = currentSimTime - delay */



40  real_T tStart,



41  real_T *tBuf,



42  real_T *uBuf,



43  int_T bufSz,



44  int_T *lastIdx,



45  int_T oldestIdx,



46  int_T newIdx,



47  real_T initOutput,



48  boolean_T discrete,



49  boolean_T minorStepAndTAtLastMajorOutput)



50{



51  int_T i;



52  real_T yout, t1, t2, u1, u2;



53



54  /*



55   * If there is only one data point in the buffer, this data point must be



56   * the t= 0 and tMinusDelay > t0, it ask for something unknown. The best



57   * guess if initial output as well



58   */



59  if ((newIdx == 0) && (oldestIdx ==0 ) && (tMinusDelay > tStart))



60    return initOutput;



61



62  /*



63   * If tMinusDelay is less than zero, should output initial value



64   */



65  if (tMinusDelay <= tStart)



66    return initOutput;



67



68  /* For fixed buffer extrapolation:



69   * if tMinusDelay is small than the time at oldestIdx, if discrete, output



70   * tailptr value,  else use tailptr and tailptr+1 value to extrapolate



71   * It is also for fixed buffer. Note: The same condition can happen for transport delay block where



72   * use tStart and and t[tail] other than using t[tail] and t[tail+1].



73   * See below



74   */



75  if ((tMinusDelay <= tBuf[oldestIdx] ) ) {



76    if (discrete) {



77      return(uBuf[oldestIdx]);



78    } else {



79      int_T tempIdx= oldestIdx + 1;



80      if (oldestIdx == bufSz-1)



81        tempIdx = 0;



82      t1= tBuf[oldestIdx];



83      t2= tBuf[tempIdx];



84      u1= uBuf[oldestIdx];



85      u2= uBuf[tempIdx];



86      if (t2 == t1) {



87        if (tMinusDelay >= t2) {



88          yout = u2;



89        } else {



90          yout = u1;



91        }



92      } else {



93        real_T f1 = (t2-tMinusDelay) / (t2-t1);



94        real_T f2 = 1.0 - f1;



95



96        /*



97         * Use Lagrange's interpolation formula.  Exact outputs at t1, t2.



98         */



99        yout = f1*u1 + f2*u2;



100      }

102      return yout;



103    }



104  }



105



106  /*



107   * When block does not have direct feedthrough, we use the table of



108   * values to extrapolate off the end of the table for delays that are less



109   * than 0 (less then step size).  This is not completely accurate.  The



110   * chain of events is as follows for a given time t.  Major output - look



111   * in table.  Update - add entry to table.  Now, if we call the output at



112   * time t again, there is a new entry in the table. For very small delays,



113   * this means that we will have a different answer from the previous call



114   * to the output fcn at the same time t.  The following code prevents this



115   * from happening.



116   */



117  if (minorStepAndTAtLastMajorOutput) {



118    /* pretend that the new entry has not been added to table */



119    if (newIdx != 0) {



120      if (*lastIdx == newIdx) {



121        (*lastIdx)--;



122      }



123



124      newIdx--;



125    } else {



126      if (*lastIdx == newIdx) {



127        *lastIdx = bufSz-1;



128      }



129



130      newIdx = bufSz - 1;



131    }



132  }



133



134  i = *lastIdx;



135  if (tBuf[i] < tMinusDelay) {



136    /* Look forward starting at last index */



137    while (tBuf[i] < tMinusDelay) {



138      /* May occur if the delay is less than step-size - extrapolate */



139      if (i == newIdx)



140        break;



141      i = ( i < (bufSz-1) ) ? (i+1) : 0;/* move through buffer */



142    }



143  } else {



144    /*



145     * Look backwards starting at last index which can happen when the



146     * delay time increases.



147     */



148    while (tBuf[i] >= tMinusDelay) {



149      /*



150       * Due to the entry condition at top of function, we



151       * should never hit the end.



152       */



153      i = (i > 0) ? i-1 : (bufSz-1);   /* move through buffer */



154    }



155



156    i = ( i < (bufSz-1) ) ? (i+1) : 0;



157  }



158



159  *lastIdx = i;



160  if (discrete) {



161    /*



162     * tempEps = 128 * eps;



163     * localEps = max(tempEps, tempEps*fabs(tBuf[i]))/2;



164     */



165    double tempEps = (DBL_EPSILON) * 128.0;



166    double localEps = tempEps * fabs(tBuf[i]);



167    if (tempEps > localEps) {



168      localEps = tempEps;



169    }



170



171    localEps = localEps / 2.0;



172    if (tMinusDelay >= (tBuf[i] - localEps)) {



173      yout = uBuf[i];



174    } else {



175      if (i == 0) {



176        yout = uBuf[bufSz-1];



177      } else {



178        yout = uBuf[i-1];



179      }



180    }



181  } else {



182    if (i == 0) {



183      t1 = tBuf[bufSz-1];



184      u1 = uBuf[bufSz-1];



185    } else {



186      t1 = tBuf[i-1];



187      u1 = uBuf[i-1];



188    }



189



190    t2 = tBuf[i];



191    u2 = uBuf[i];



192    if (t2 == t1) {



193      if (tMinusDelay >= t2) {



194        yout = u2;



195      } else {



196        yout = u1;



197      }



198    } else {



199      real_T f1 = (t2-tMinusDelay) / (t2-t1);



200      real_T f2 = 1.0 - f1;

202      /*



203       * Use Lagrange's interpolation formula.  Exact outputs at t1, t2.



204       */



205      yout = f1*u1 + f2*u2;



206    }



207  }



208



209  return(yout);

339void rt_invd5x5_snf(const real_T u[25], real_T y[25])



340{

344  int8_T ipiv[5];



345  int32_T j;

348  real_T s;

353  int32_T i_0;

355    y[i_0] = 0.0;



356    A[i_0] = u[i_0];



357  }



358



359  for (i_0 = 0; i_0 < 5; i_0++) {



360    ipiv[i_0] = (int8_T)(1 + i_0);



361  }



362



363  for (j = 0; j < 4; j++) {



364    c = j * 6;



365    kAcol = j * 6;



366    jBcol = 1;



367    ix = c;



368    smax = fabs(A[kAcol]);



369    for (jA = 2; jA <= 5 - j; jA++) {



370      ix++;



371      s = fabs(A[ix]);



372      if (s > smax) {



373        jBcol = jA;



374        smax = s;



375      }



376    }



377



378    jBcol--;



379    if (A[c + jBcol] != 0.0) {



380      if (jBcol != 0) {



381        ipiv[j] = (int8_T)((j + jBcol) + 1);



382        ix = j;



383        jBcol += j;



384        for (jA = 0; jA < 5; jA++) {



385          smax = A[ix];



386          A[ix] = A[jBcol];



387          A[jBcol] = smax;



388          ix += 5;



389          jBcol += 5;



390        }



391      }



392



393      i_0 = c - j;



394      for (i = c + 1; i + 1 <= i_0 + 5; i++) {



395        A[i] /= A[c];



396      }



397    }



398



399    jA = kAcol;



400    jBcol = kAcol + 5;



401    for (kAcol = 1; kAcol <= 4 - j; kAcol++) {



402      if (A[jBcol] != 0.0) {



403        smax = -A[jBcol];



404        ix = c;



405        i_0 = jA - j;



406        for (i = jA + 6; i + 1 <= i_0 + 10; i++) {



407          A[i] += A[ix + 1] * smax;



408          ix++;



409        }



410      }



411



412      jBcol += 5;



413      jA += 5;



414    }



415  }



416



417  for (i_0 = 0; i_0 < 5; i_0++) {



418    p[i_0] = (int8_T)(1 + i_0);



419  }



420



421  if (ipiv[0] > 1) {



422    jBcol = p[ipiv[0] - 1];



423    p[ipiv[0] - 1] = p[0];



424    p[0] = (int8_T)jBcol;



425  }



426



427  if (ipiv[1] > 2) {



428    jBcol = p[ipiv[1] - 1];



429    p[ipiv[1] - 1] = p[1];



430    p[1] = (int8_T)jBcol;



431  }



432



433  if (ipiv[2] > 3) {



434    jBcol = p[ipiv[2] - 1];



435    p[ipiv[2] - 1] = p[2];



436    p[2] = (int8_T)jBcol;



437  }



438



439  if (ipiv[3] > 4) {



440    jBcol = p[ipiv[3] - 1];



441    p[ipiv[3] - 1] = p[3];



442    p[3] = (int8_T)jBcol;



443  }



444



445  for (jA = 0; jA < 5; jA++) {



446    c = p[jA] - 1;



447    y[jA + 5 * (p[jA] - 1)] = 1.0;



448    for (j = jA; j + 1 < 6; j++) {



449      if (y[5 * c + j] != 0.0) {



450        for (i = j + 1; i + 1 < 6; i++) {



451          y[i + 5 * c] -= y[5 * c + j] * A[5 * j + i];



452        }



453      }



454    }



455  }



456



457  for (j = 0; j < 5; j++) {



458    jBcol = 5 * j;



459    for (jA = 4; jA >= 0; jA += -1) {



460      kAcol = 5 * jA;



461      if (y[jA + jBcol] != 0.0) {



462        y[jA + jBcol] /= A[jA + kAcol];



463        for (i = 0; i + 1 <= jA; i++) {



464          y[i + jBcol] -= y[jA + jBcol] * A[i + kAcol];



465        }



466      }



467    }



468  }

471real_T rt_hypotd_snf(real_T u0, real_T u1)



472{



473  real_T y;



474  real_T a;



475  a = fabs(u0);



476  y = fabs(u1);



477  if (a < y) {



478    a /= y;



479    y *= sqrt(a * a + 1.0);



480  } else if (a > y) {



481    y /= a;



482    y = sqrt(y * y + 1.0) * a;



483  } else {



484    if (!rtIsNaN(y)) {



485      y = a * 1.4142135623730951;



486    }



487  }



488



489  return y;



490}

496  int32_T u1_0;

504    }

507      u1_0 = 1;

521  } else {

1199                break;

1299                      }



1300                    }



1301                  }



1302                }



1303              }



1304            }



1305          }



1306        }                              /* if (swChanged) */

1308

2923      SimStruct *rts = Diesel_DER_M->childSfunctions[5];



2924      sfcnUpdate(rts, 1);



2925      if (ssGetErrorStatus(rts) != (NULL))



2926        return;



2927    }



2928



2929    /* Update for UnitDelay: '<S105>/Unit Delay' */



2930    Diesel_DER_DW.UnitDelay_DSTATE_ch = rtb_Product1_e;



2931



2932    /* Update for UnitDelay: '<S105>/Unit Delay1' */



2933    Diesel_DER_DW.UnitDelay1_DSTATE_j = rtb_Switch_of;



2934



2935    /* Update for UnitDelay: '<S133>/voltages' incorporates:



2936     *  Constant: '<S118>/[ Vkd =0 Vkq1=0  Vkq2=0 ]'



2937     */



2938    Diesel_DER_DW.voltages_DSTATE_h[0] = rtb_Fcn2_p;



2939    Diesel_DER_DW.voltages_DSTATE_h[1] = rtb_Fcn3_o;



2940    Diesel_DER_DW.voltages_DSTATE_h[2] = rtb_Vfd_o;



2941    Diesel_DER_DW.voltages_DSTATE_h[3] = Diesel_DER_P.Vkd0Vkq10Vkq20_Value_a[0];



2942    Diesel_DER_DW.voltages_DSTATE_h[4] = Diesel_DER_P.Vkd0Vkq10Vkq20_Value_a[1];



2943



2944    /* Update for DiscreteIntegrator: '<S120>/Rotor speed deviation (dw)' */



2945    Diesel_DER_DW.Rotorspeeddeviationdw_SYSTEM_EN = 0U;



2946    Diesel_DER_DW.Rotorspeeddeviationdw_DSTATE =



2947      Diesel_DER_P.Rotorspeeddeviationdw_gainval * rtb_uH + Diesel_DER_B.dw;



2948



2949    /* Update for DiscreteIntegrator: '<S112>/Integ4' */



2950    Diesel_DER_DW.Integ4_SYSTEM_ENABLE_l = 0U;



2951    Diesel_DER_DW.Integ4_DSTATE_i = Diesel_DER_P.Integ4_gainval_k *



2952      rtb_UnitDelay4 + Diesel_DER_B.Integ4_j;



2953



2954    /* Level2 S-Function Block: '<S113>/S-Function' (sfun_discreteVariableDelay) */



2955    {



2956      SimStruct *rts = Diesel_DER_M->childSfunctions[6];



2957      sfcnUpdate(rts, 1);



2958      if (ssGetErrorStatus(rts) != (NULL))



2959        return;



2960    }



2961



2962    /* Update for UnitDelay: '<S147>/Delay Ts' */



2963    Diesel_DER_DW.DelayTs_DSTATE = Diesel_DER_B.StateSpace_o1[0];



2964



2965    /* Update for UnitDelay: '<S147>/Delay Ts ' */



2966    Diesel_DER_DW.DelayTs_DSTATE_f = rtb_Sum_k;



2967



2968    /* Update for UnitDelay: '<S150>/Delay Ts' */



2969    Diesel_DER_DW.DelayTs_DSTATE_a = Diesel_DER_B.StateSpace_o1[1];



2970



2971    /* Update for UnitDelay: '<S150>/Delay Ts ' */



2972    Diesel_DER_DW.DelayTs_DSTATE_n = rtb_Sum_o;



2973



2974    /* Update for UnitDelay: '<S153>/Delay Ts' */



2975    Diesel_DER_DW.DelayTs_DSTATE_l = Diesel_DER_B.StateSpace_o1[2];



2976



2977    /* Update for UnitDelay: '<S153>/Delay Ts ' */



2978    Diesel_DER_DW.DelayTs_DSTATE_d = rtb_Sum_b;



2979  }



2980



2981  /* Update absolute time for base rate */



2982  /* The "clockTick0" counts the number of times the code of this task has



2983   * been executed. The absolute time is the multiplication of "clockTick0"



2984   * and "Timing.stepSize0". Size of "clockTick0" ensures timer will not



2985   * overflow during the application lifespan selected.



2986   */



2987  Diesel_DER_M->Timing.t[0] =



2988    (++Diesel_DER_M->Timing.clockTick0) * Diesel_DER_M->Timing.stepSize0;



2989



2990  {



2991    /* Update absolute timer for sample time: [5.0E-5s, 0.0s] */



2992    /* The "clockTick1" counts the number of times the code of this task has



2993     * been executed. The absolute time is the multiplication of "clockTick1"



2994     * and "Timing.stepSize1". Size of "clockTick1" ensures timer will not



2995     * overflow during the application lifespan selected.



2996     */



2997    Diesel_DER_M->Timing.t[1] =



2998      (++Diesel_DER_M->Timing.clockTick1) * Diesel_DER_M->Timing.stepSize1;



2999  }



3000}
